---
layout: paradigm
paradigm: ADJ_OPAAKKI
---
### ` ADJ_OPAAKKI `

* _kki stems, kki : ke variations_
* Universal POS is ADJ and legacy POS is ADJECTIVE
* suffixes use back vowel harmony
* KOTUS paradigm used in their dictionary is 5-A
* The lemmas must end in * ki * (which will be deleted to form an invariant stub) and the regex matching the lemma is ` [AOUŌÓÅaouåôąáăâāóōúūû][^äöy]*kki `
